4. Errors and Fixes:

   - **Error 1: Anthropic API 404 - Model Not Found**
     - **Description**: `404 {"type":"error","error":{"type":"not_found_error","message":"model: claude-3-5-sonnet-20241022"}}`
     - **How fixed**: Updated model configuration in both `semantic-analysis-agent.ts` and `semantic-analyzer.ts` to use `claude-sonnet-4-20250514` and increased max_tokens to 4096
     - **Result**: API calls now succeed and generate real LLM insights (1393 characters vs 597 characters of rule-based fallback)
     - **User feedback**: None - I discovered this issue during incremental agent testing

   - **Error 2: VkbApiClient Module Not Found**
     - **Description**: `Cannot find module '/Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/integrations/mcp-server-semantic-analysis/dist/lib/ukb-unified/core/VkbApiClient.js' imported from /Users/<USER_ID_REDACTED>/Agentic/coding/integrations/mcp-server-semantic-analysis/dist/integrations/mcp-server-semantic-analysis/src/storage/graph-database-adapter.js`
     - **Root cause**: Relative import path `../../../../lib/ukb-unified/core/VkbApiClient.js` didn't resolve correctly after TypeScript compilation to nested dist structure
     - **How fixed**: Changed to construct absolute path from dbPath parameter: `const repoRoot = this.dbPath.replace(/\/.data\/knowledge-graph$/, ''); const vkbClientPath = \`${repoRoot}/lib/ukb-unified/core/VkbApiClient.js\`;`
     - **Result**: GraphDB adapter successfully initializes using VKB API (lock-free mode)
     - **User feedback**: None - I discovered and fixed this issue during testing

   - **Error 3: Workflow Method Names Incorrect**
     - **Description**: `Action analyzeRecentChanges not found on agent git_history. Available methods: analyzeGitHistory, validateGitRepository, getLastAnalysisCheckpoint, saveAnalysisCheckpoint, extractCommits, parseGitLogOutput, ...`
     - **Root cause**: Workflow definition in coordinator.ts was calling methods that don't exist on the agents
     - **How fixed**: Updated workflow step method names:
       - `analyzeRecentChanges` ‚Üí `analyzeGitHistory`
       - `analyzeRecentVibes` ‚Üí `analyzeVibeHistory`
       - `persistIncremental` ‚Üí `persistAnalysisResults`
     - **Result**: Workflow successfully routes to correct agent methods
     - **User feedback**: None - I discovered this issue during full workflow testing

   - **Error 4: MCP Server Running Old Code**
     - **Description**: After committing fixes, calling `mcp__semantic-analysis__execute_workflow` still returned the old error about `analyzeRecentChanges`
     - **Root cause**: MCP server process (PID 82907) was still running with old compiled code, hadn't restarted to pick up changes
     - **How fixed**: Killed the MCP server process with `kill 82907` to force restart
     - **Result**: MCP server disconnected (restarting), workflow test returned "Not connected" error
     - **User feedback**: User requested to test via `ukb` command, which triggered this discovery
